07/20/2014 22:27:19 - This library is good to go. This is no surprise, since the
                      changes, save one, are in WizardWrx.DLLServices2.dll, for
                      which this program is essentially an extension of its test
                      stand.
                      
                      The fact that the test stand for this library covers uses
                      cases for WizardWrx.DLLServices2.dll is the result of them
                      being developed initially as part of its deprecated
                      predecessor, WizardWrx.ConsoleAppAids.dll. I moved them to
                      WizardWrx.DLLServices2.dll to unravel a circular 
                      dependency that made testing of that library and its
                      twin, WizardWrx.ApplicationHelpers.dll, almost impossible.
                      Moving some routines into WizardWrx.DLLServices2.dll broke
                      the codependency.
                      
                      Since I expect all three libraries to stabilize and remain
                      pretty much as they are today, I decided to leave the test
                      cases where they were.
